\bentry
\word[I(1)]{I, i}
\pron{ai}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{Is} yA \eng{I's}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} iMgilxSf vaNaRmAleya oMbatatxneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} (roVmanf aMkanadalilx) = \eng{1;} `oMdu' \eng{(I, i = 1, ii = 2, ix = 9, cii = 102).} 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[I(2)]{I}
\pron{ai}
\gl{\sanA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{we;}}
\bmng
 divxtiVyA viBakitx \eng{me} \ucAcx\ mi, yA otutx hAkidAga mI; \AtAmx\ \eng{myself,} \pArxparx\ \eng{me}, \bava\ \eng{we;} SaSiThxV viBakitx \eng{my, mine,} \bava\ \eng{our}). 
\bnum
\num{1} \Eva\ \sanA\ parxthama puruSa \eng{me,} (\AmA); (udAgxragaLalilx) \eng{ah me}!, \eng{dear me}!, \eng{silly me}! 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[ice(1)]{ice}
\pron{aisf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} aisu; niVgaRlulx; niVgaRDeDx; maMjugaDeDx; GaniVBavisida niVru. 
\num{2} niVrina meVle teVluva maMjugaDeDxya hALe. 
\num{3} maMjugaDeDx miThAyi yA adara tuMDu, \kanmu (\birx) aisfkirxVmf yA aisf peVDa. 
\num{4} (\ashi) vajarxgaLu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{dry ice} Gana iMgAlada DeYAkesxYDu. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{break the ice} 
\banum
\alnum{a} AraMBa mADu; shuru mADu. 
\alnum{b} bigumAnavanunx biDu; shirxVmadAgxMBiVyaRvanunx tore. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \hyperref{kandict_c.pdf}{C}{cut(2) nuga(21)}{$^2$cuts no ice.} 
\numi{3} \eng{on ice} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (ATa, vinoVda, \mo vugaLa \vi) (himatalada meVle) jArugaru, sekxVTarugaLu-mADida. 
\alnum{b} (\AmA) tAtAkxlikavAgi-sathxgitagoLisiruva, nilugaDeyalilx(TiTx)ruva, taDehiDidiruva. 
\alnum{c} (\AmA) KaDAKaMDitavAda; KacitavAda. 
\hyperdef{I}{ice(1) nuga(4)}{} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} \eng{on thin ice} atisUkaSxmX parisithxtiyalilx; aBadarx sithxtiyalilx; apAyadalilx: \eng{you are on thin ice with that argument} A vAdavanunx hiDidare ninanx sithxti aBadarx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[if(1)]{if}
\pron{iphf}
\gl{\saMavayx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} -re; -idadxre; -idadxlilx; -Adalilx; -pakaSxkekx; -pakaSxdalilx: \eng{if you are tired} niVnu baLalidadxre. \eng{if you (hereafter) see him, give him the message} avanu ninage (muMde) sikakxre I sudidx koDu. 
\num{2} (asaMBavavAda saMdaBaRvanunx sUcisuvalilx yAvudeV dhAtuvina BUtarUpadoDane) -- oMdu veVLe Adare, idadxre, naDedare: \eng{if I were you} nAneV niVnAgididxdadxre; ninanx sAthxnadalilx yA sithxtiyalilx nAnu ididxdadxre. \eng{if he came tomorrow} nALe avanu oMdu veVLe baMdare. 
\num{3} yAvAga; eMdAdarU; yAvAgalAdarU: \eng{if I feel any doubt} yAvAgalAdarU nanage saMshaya baMdare. 
\num{4} -yoV; -yeV; -vudeV; sAdhayxveV: \eng{see if you can turn the handle} hiDiyanunx tirugisalu ninage AgutatxdeyeV noVDu. 
\numi{5} 
\banum
\alnum{a} \eng{if} padavanunx biTuTxbiTATxga kirxyApadavu kataqR padakekx modaleV barutatxde, \udA: \eng{were in your place (= if I were in your place). would, could, should, might, had he (= if he would, could, should, might, had).} 
\alnum{b} (\kAparx) \eng{loved I not honour more = if I loved not honour more.} 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} (bayake, AshacxyaR, \mo vugaLa udAgxragaLalilx vAkayxda anugata BAgavilalxde): \eng{if I only knew}! nanage tiLididadxre (eSuTx cenAnxgitutx)! \eng{if I haven't lost my watch}! nananx gaDiyAravanunx nAnu kaLedukoLaLxdidadxre! (kaLedukoMDenalAlx eMba AshacxyaRda yA beVsarada dhavxni). 
\num{7} (vinayadiMda beVDuvAga) \eng{if you wouldn't mind opening the door?} niVnu EnU tiLidukoLaLxdidadxre dayamADi bAgilu tegeyuveyA? 
\num{8} AdarU; hAgidadxrU; AdAgUyx: \eng{a useful if cumbersome device} toDakinadAdarU upayukatx salakaraNe. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{as if} -hAge; -aMte; -heVgoV hAge: \eng{it seems as if he meant} (ADumAtinalilx \eng{means} eMdu \parx) \eng{to compromise} avanige rAjimADikoLuLxva aBipArxyavidadx hAge toVrutatxde. \eng{he talks as if he were drunk} avanu kuDididadxre heVge mAtanADutitxdadxnoV hAge (yA kuDididadxre heVgoV hAge) mAtanADutAtxne. \eng{as if you didn't know} ninage EnU gotitxlalxdidadxMte (ninage cenAnxgi gotutx eMba dhavxni). 
\num{2} \eng{if and when} (Aguva saMBavavidadxre) AdAga; hAgAdAga; muMde; BaviSayxdalilx. 
\hypertarget{if nuga3}{} 
\num{3} \eng{if any} yAvudAdarU yA yAvuvAdarU idadxlilx. 
\num{4} \eng{if anything} = \hyperlink{if nuga3}{?nuga? \((3)\)}. 
\numi{5} \eng{if at all} 
\banum
\alnum{a} pArxyashaH ilalxveV ilalx. 
\alnum{b} aMtAdarU, hAgAdarU -- ilalx. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{6} \eng{if not} hAgiradidadxre; aMtiradidadxlilx. 
\hypertarget{if nuga7}{} 
\num{7} \eng{if only because} (beVre yAvudeV kAraNakAkxgi AgadidadxrU) A kAraNakAkxgi; adakAkxgi. 
\num{8} \eng{if only to} = \hyperlink{if nuga7}{?nuga? \((7)\)}.

\bentry
\word[ill(1)]{ill}
\pron{ilf}
\gl{\gu}
\expl{(\tara\ \eng{worse,} \tama\ \eng{worst}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (\sA\ AKAyxtaka \parx) beVne bidadx; anAroVgayxda; asavxsathx; kAyileya; roVgiSaThx; roVgavuLaLx: \eng{he was ill} avanige kAyileyAyitu. \eng{he was taken ill with (of) disease} avanige A beVneyiMda anAroVgayxvAyitu. \eng{ill with anxiety etc.} ciMte \mo vugaLiMda beVne hiDida. 
\num{2} (AroVgayxda \vi) neTaTxgilalxda; sariyAgilalxda; keTuTxhoVda. 
\num{3} aneYtika; niVtigeTaTx; shiVlageTaTx; aniVtiya: \eng{ill fame} keTaTx hesaru; duyaRshasusx. 
\num{4} devxVSada; hagetanadiMda kUDida: \eng{ill blood, ill feeling, ill will} devxVSa, hagetana. 
\num{5} hAnikara; apAyakara; keDuku mADuva: \eng{ill effects} duSapxriNAmagaLu. 
\num{6} hALAda; hiVna; aniSaTx; daridarx; anathaRda; anAhutada: \eng{ill fortune} hiVna adaqSaTx. 
\num{7} (\pArxparx) kaSaTxvAda; parxyAsada: \eng{ill to please} mecicxsalu kaSaTxvAda. 
\num{8} doVSadiMda kUDida; loVpavuLaLx. 
\num{9} jANemxyilalxda; caturateyilalxda; anipuNa; akushala: \eng{ill taste} duSATxBiruci. \eng{ill management} akushala nivaRhaNe. 
\num{10} (mayARde yA naDavaLikeya \vi) taravalalxda; tagada; salalxda; ayoVgayx; ayukatx; anucita. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\nuga}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{do an ill turn to (person)} (vayxkitxge yA avana hitakekx) keDuku mADu; keVDu mADu; hAni taru. 
\num{2} \eng{fall (}\engit{or} \eng{be taken) ill} kAyile biVLu. 
\num{3} \eng{ill weeds grow apace} keTaTx kaLe balu beVga beLeyutatxde; hAnikaravAdudu bahaLa beVga haraDutatxde yA beLeyutatxde. 
\num{4} \eng{it's an ill wind that blows nobody good} yArigU oLeLxyadanunx mADada saMgati nijavAgiyU bahaLa keTaTxdudx. 
\num{5} \eng{with an ill grace} muKa gaMTu hAkikoMDu; asamAdhAnadiMda; aparxsananxteyiMda. 
\enum
\emng

\num{3} beLaku niVDike; parxkAshana; parxkAshagoLisuvike: \eng{the brilliant illumination of the room} koThaDiya ujajxvXla parxkAshana. 
\num{4} diVpAlaMkAra: \eng{illumination of the city in celebration of the victory} vijayoVtasxvakAkxgi nagarada diVpAlaMkAra. 
\num{5} (hasatxparxtiya) suvaNARlaMkaraNa; hasatxparxtiya akaSxra \mo vanunx cinanx, beLiLx yA itara ujajxvXla vaNaRgaLiMda alaMkarisuvudu: \eng{interested in the illumination of manuscripts} hasatxparxtigaLa suvaNARlaMkaraNadalilx AsakatxnAda.

\bentry
\word[in(1)]{in}
\pron{inf}
\gl{\upa}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} -- alilx: 
\banum
\alnum{a} deVsha, kAla, saMdaBaR, \mo vugaLa parimitigaLige oLapaTiTxruvudanonxV, avugaLalilx vayxkitxya yA vasutxvina sAthxnavanonxV nideRVshisuvalilx. 
\alnum{b} KaMDa, deVsha, doDaDx yA parxsidadhx nagaragaLa \vi: \eng{in Asia} ESAyxdalilx, \eng{in India} BAratadalilx. \eng{in Mysore} meYsUrinalilx.

\bnum

\num{3} (satAyxMshavanunx heVLuvalilx) nijavAgi; vAsatxvavAgi: \eng{if indeed such a thing is possible} nijavAgi aMtha oMdu viSaya sAdhayxvAda pakaSxdalilx. \eng{saw here recently, indeed yesterday} ititxVcege noVDide, nijavAgi nenenx. 
\num{4} (obabxra mAtanunx samathiRsuvAga yA vayxMgayxvAgi nirAkarisuvAga) nijavAgi: \eng{who is this Mr. Rao? who is he, indeed}! I rAvf yAru? nijavAgi, avaru yAru! (hAgeMdu keVLabahudeV ?) 
\num{5} (mAtina athaRda oMdu aMshavanunx opipxkoLuLxvAga) nijavAgi: \eng{there are indeed exceptions} apavAdagaLive, nija. 
\num{6} (parxshAnxthaRkavAgi) hwdeV ? hAgeyeV? nijaveV? : \eng{``that's Ram.'' ``Indeed?''} ``avanu rAma.'' ``hwdeV?''

\bentry

\gl{\gu}
\bmng

\num{3} vayxkitx sAvxtaMtarxyXvAdiya. 
\num{4} veYyakitxka; vayxkitx veYshiSaTxyXda; vayxkitx veYlakaSxNayxgaLiMda kUDida: \eng{strongly individualistic tendencies} tiVra veYyakitxka parxvaqtitxgaLu. 
\enum
\emng

\alnum{a} parxveVshadAvxra; parxveVsha yoVjane; parxveVshasAdhana; mAhiti, \mo vu oMdu vayxvasethxyanunx parxveVshisuva sathxLa, EpARTu yA sAdhana.

\bentry
\word{intend}
\pron{iMTeMDf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} udedxVshisu; iciCxsu; bayasu; saMkalipxsu; gurihoMdiru; bage; kuri: \eng{we intend no harm} keVDu mADabeVkeMbudu namamx udedxVshavalalx. \eng{was this intended?} idanunx udedxVshapaTuTx mADalAyiteV? 
\numi{2} (\BUkaq dalilx) 
\banum

\alnum{b} udedxVshadiMda mADida; udedxVshapUvaRkavAda. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (\vakaq dalilx) udedxVshisu; baralu, mADalu -- udedxVshaviru, iSaTxpaDu: \eng{an intending visitor} BeVTiya udedxVshaviruvavanu. 
\num{4} (yAvudAdarU vasutxvanunx, vayxkitxyanunx oMdu udedxVsha \mo vakekx) udedxVshisu; iDu; tegediDu; kAdirisu; mIsalAgiDu; gotutx mADu; ujujxgisu; tayArisu; niyoVjisu: \eng{we intend our son for the Bar} namamx maga lAyarf AgaleMdu udedxVshisidedxVve. \eng{this fruit is intended for you} I haNaNxnunx ninagAgi iTiTxde. \eng{this daub is intended for me} I baNaNxda boTuTx nanagAgi ide (nananxnunx parxtinidhisutatxde, nananxnunx saMkeVtisutatxde). 
\num{5} aBipArxyapaDu; athaRniVDu: \eng{what exactly do you intend by the word?} I padakekx KacitavAgi ninanx athaRveVnu?

\emng

\pron{iMTarfbelxMDf}
\gl{\sakirx}
\bmng
(oMdaroDane inonxMdanunx) seVrisu; beresu; kalasu; saMmisharxmADu; milAyisu. 
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
(oMdaroDane) seVru; bere; kale; saMmisharxvAgu; milAyisu. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{interbreed}
\pron{iMTarfbirxVDf}
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{interbred}).}
\bmng
 \sakirx (BinanxvaMshada pArxNigaLa yA sasayxgaLa \vi) taLi berasu; taLi -- misharx mADu, saMkarisu; aDaDxtaLi beLasu; saMkaroVtapxtitx mADisu. 
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\akirx}
\bmng
(beVre beVre vaMshada manuSayxru, pArxNigaLu yA sasayxgaLu) parasapxra bere; saMkaroVtapxtitxyAgu yA saMkaroVtapxtitxmADu. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{intercalary}
\pron{iMTarfka(kAYx)lari}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (dina yA tiMgaLina \vi) adhika; cAMdarxmAnada vaSaRvanunx swramAnada vaSaRkekx sari hoMdisuvudakAkxgi naDuve seVrisida (\udA\ adhika vaSaRdalilx baruva Pebarxvari \eng{29}neV tAriVKu): \eng{intercalary month} adhika mAsa. 
\num{2} (vaSaRda \vi) adhika; adhika dina yA adhikamAsa uLaLx. 
\num{3} naDuve, madheyx -- seVrisida; parxkiSxpatx; aMtaHkiSxpatx; naDuve tUrisida; aMtaniRviSaTx. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\expl{}
\bmng

\num{2} (badalAvaNe, sithxti, pariNAma -- ivanunx tiLisuvAga) oMdakekx; rUpakekx; rUpavAgi: \eng{turn stones into gold} kalulxgaLanunx cinanxkekx, honinxge -- tirugisu. \eng{translate into English} iMgilxSige BASAMtarisu. \eng{grow into an adult} vayasakxnAgi beLe. \eng{collect them into heaps} avanunx rAshigaLAgi sheVKarisu. \eng{divide them into three classes} avanunx mUru vagaRgaLAgi viBAgisu. \eng{flogged into submission} sharaNAguvaMte, sharaNAguvavaregU koraDiniMda baDidu. 
\num{3} (\AmA) Asakitxyiruva; tiLidiruva: \eng{is really into art} nijavAgiyU kaleyalilx Asakitxyide.

\num{1} oLage taru; parxveVshagoLisu; oLakekx taru. 
\num{2} oLagiDu; oLakikxDu; oLahogisu; oLakekx seVrisu. 
\num{3} (padadhxti, BAvane, sudhAraNe, \mo vanunx) baLakege, cAlitxge, jArige, rUDhige, AcaraNege taru. 
\num{4} (viSaya \mo vanunx) muMdoDuDx; maMDisu; sUcisu; muMdiDu. 
\num{5} upakarxmisu; pArxraMBisu. 
\num{6} muMdAgu; AraMBadalilxru; yAvudeV oMdu AraMBavAguvudakekx munanx Agu, jarugu. 
\num{7} (obabxnanunx inonxbabxnige, \kanmu\ sAMparxdAyika riVtiyalilx) paricayagoLisu; paricaya mADikoDu. 
\num{8} (variSaThxvagaRda taruNiyanunx) ADhayx samAjakekx -- vidhuyxkatxvAgi paricayagoLisu, parxveVshagoLisu. 
\num{9} (parxkaqta viSayakekx modalabArige obabxna) gamana seLe, harisu. 
\num{10} (masUde \mo vanunx) shAsanasaBeyalilx maMDisu; saMsatitxnalilx taru. 
\num{11} (AkAshavANiya kAyaRkarxma \mo vanunx) shorxVtaqgaLa, viVkaSxkara eduru parxdashiRsu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{introduction}
\pron{infTarxDakfSanf}
\gl{\nA}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} parxveVshana; oLage, oLakekx taruvudu. 
\num{2} aMtaniRveVshana; oLage, oLakekx iDuvudu, seVrisuvudu; oLahogisuvudu. 
\num{3} oLakekx seVrisida -- vasutx, viSaya. 
\num{4} (padadhxti, BAvane, sudhAraNe, \mo vanunx) baLakege, AcaraNege taruvudu; cAlitxgoLisuvudu. 
\num{5} (viSaya \mo vanunx) muMdiDuvudu; muMdoDuDxvudu; sUcisuvudu; maMDisuvudu; maMDane. 
\num{6} (pusatxka, BASaNa, \mo vugaLa pArxraMBadalilx mADuva yA seVrisuva) parxsAtxvane; upoVdAvxta; BUmike; piVThike; viSayada paricaya. 
\num{7} keYpiDi; viSayavanunx paricaya mADikoDuva pArxthamika garxMtha. 
\num{8} (obabxnanunx inonxbabxnige) vidhuyxkatxvAgi paricaya mADikoDuvudu; vidhuyxkatx paricaya, sAMparxdAyika paricaya. 
\num{9} (variSaThxvagaRda taruNiyanunx) ADhayx samAjakekx paricayisuvudu, parxveVshagoLisuvudu. 
\num{10} (masUde \mo vanunx) shAsanasaBeyalilx -- maMDisuvudu; maMDane. 
\hypertarget{introduction(11)}{} 
\num{11} paricaya patarx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\bmng
\eng{letter of introduction} = \hyperlink{introduction(11)}{introduction(11)}. 
\emng

\bentry
\word{inventive}
\pron{infveMTivf}
\gl{\gu}
\bmng

\bentry
\word[it(1)]{it}
\pron{iTf}
\gl{\sanA}
\bmng
(SaSiThxV viBakitx \eng{its}; \bava\ \eng{they}, divxtiVyA viBakitx \eng{them}, SaSiThxV viBakitx \eng{their}). 
\bnum
\num{1} adu; idu; parxsakatx viSaya, vasutx (kelavomemx liMga tiLiyada yA liMga aBiperxVtavAgirada pArxNi yA magu): \eng{took a stone and threw it} oMdu kalulx tegedukoMDu adanunx eseda. 
\num{2} parxsutxta vayxkitx: \eng{who is it that knocks?} adu yAru, bAgilu taTuTxvavanu? \eng{it is I} (adu) nAnu. \eng{is it a boy or a girl?} adu huDuganoV, huDugiyoV? 
\num{3} (\pArxparx, \kAparx) manasasxnunx vAyxpisiruvudu, tuMbiruvudu: \eng{it is the miller's daughter} giraNi mAlikana magaLu nananx manasasxnunx vAyxpisidAdxLe. 
\num{4} BAvavAcaka kirxyApadagaLa kataqRvAgi: \eng{it rains} maLe hoyuyxtatxde. \eng{it is cold} taNaNxgide. \eng{it is winter} (adu, idu) caLigAla. \eng{it is 6 miles to the village} haLiLxge Aru meYli (dUra) Agutatxde. \eng{it is Wednesday today} iMdu budhavAra. \eng{it says in the Bible} beYbalf ( -- eMdu) heVLutatxde. \eng{I would go if it were not for the expense} vecacxvilalxdidadxre nAnu hoVgutitxdedx. 
\num{5} muMde baruva nijavAda kataqRvanunx pUvaRBAviyAgi sUcisuva gwNa kataqRvAgi: \eng{it is absurd talking (to talk) like that} hAge mAtADuvudu asaMgata. \eng{it is incredible that he should refuse} avanu nirAkarisidaneMbudu naMbalu asAdhayx. 
\num{6} (\kirxvi\ AKAyxtadiMda parxteyxVkagoMDiruva, \eng{that} eMba saMbaMdhAvayxyadiMda pArxraMBavAgi muMde baruva kataqRvanunx pUvaRBAviyAgi sUcisuva): \eng{it is seldom that he fails} avanu tapipxsikoLuLxvudu viraLa. 
\num{7} (\eng{that} eMba) saMbaMdhAvayxyadiMda pArxraMBavAgi muMde baruva kamaRpadavanunx pUvaRBAviyAgi sUcisuva padavAgi: \eng{see to it that they obey} avaru pAlisuvaMte noVDiko. \eng{I take it that you agree} niVnu samamxtisutitxVyeMdu nAnu garxhisutetxVne. 
\num{8} (saMbaMdhasUcakakekx pUvaRgAmi padavAgi): \eng{it was a purse that he dropped} avanu biVLisidudx oMdu haNada ciVla. 
\num{9} (\sakirx\ yA \akirx doDane anideRVshaka kamaRpadavAgi) \eng{face it out} dheYyaRdiMda edurisu. \eng{carry it with a high hand} dapaRdiMda sAdhisu. \eng{deuce take it} adu hALAgali. \eng{run for it} tavxre mADu. \eng{lord it over him} avana meVle adhikAra naDesu. \eng{cab it} (rUDhiyAgi yA nidiRSaTx saMdaBaRdalilx) kAyxbf baMDiyalilx hoVgu. \eng{give it him (hot)} bisimuTiTxsu. \eng{have done it} aviveVka mADide. 
\num{10} (\AmA) sAdhane \mo vugaLa tutatxtudi; shiKara; paramAvadhi: \eng{for barefaced lying you really are it} nAcikeyilalxde suLuLx heVLuvudaralilx niVnu nijavAgi nisisxVma, tutatxtudi muTiTxdidxVye. 
\num{11} (\AmA) leYMgika AkaSaRNe yA saMBoVga. 
\num{12} (makakxLa ATagaLalilx) itararanunx hiDiyabeVkAda ATagAra. 
\enum
